I have lived in Jincheng Courtyard for at least a dozen times in the past few years, and I have never been disappointed every time. I was lazy before and didn't write a good review for it, but I am sure of it in my heart. I remember last year, I was injured in my foot and checked in with a cane. I am very picky about service work, but the service of Zenyi Jincheng Courtyard is impeccable.
